          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;

          flex-grow: 1;

          align-items: stretch;

          flex-wrap: nowrap;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          padding-top: 0.5em;
        }
        .container-outside {
          box-sizing: border-box;
          width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        <p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





CRAS server provides a D-Bus service for the browser to use the audio. Among the methods in the D-Bus Control interface, a method called SetGlobalOutputChannelRemix receives two parameters:



<span class="line"><!---->CRAS server provides a D-Bus service for the browser to use the audio. Among the methods in the D-Bus Control interface, a method called SetGlobalOutputChannelRemix receives two parameters:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





<method name="SetGlobalOutputChannelRemix">



<span class="line"><!---->&lt;method name="SetGlobalOutputChannelRemix"&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





  <tp:docstring>



<span class="line"><!---->  &lt;tp:docstring&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





    Sets the conversion matrix for global output channel



<span class="line"><!---->    Sets the conversion matrix for global output channel<!----></span>



<br>





    remixing. The coefficient array represents an N * N



<span class="line"><!---->    remixing. The coefficient array represents an N * N<!----></span>



<br>





    conversion matrix M, where N is num_channels, with



<span class="line"><!---->    conversion matrix M, where N is num_channels, with<!----></span>



<br>





    M[i][j] = coefficient[i * N + j].



<span class="line"><!---->    M[i][j] = coefficient[i * N + j].<!----></span>



<br>





    The remix is done by multiplying the conversion matrix



<span class="line"><!---->    The remix is done by multiplying the conversion matrix<!----></span>



<br>





    to each N-channel PCM data, i.e M * [L, R] = [L', R']



<span class="line"><!---->    to each N-channel PCM data, i.e M * [L, R] = [L', R']<!----></span>



<br>





    For example, coefficient [0.1, 0.9, 0.4, 0.6] will



<span class="line"><!---->    For example, coefficient [0.1, 0.9, 0.4, 0.6] will<!----></span>



<br>





    result in:



<span class="line"><!---->    result in:<!----></span>



<br>





    L' = 0.1 * L + 0.9 * R



<span class="line"><!---->    L' = 0.1 * L + 0.9 * R<!----></span>



<br>





    R' = 0.4 * L + 0.6 * R



<span class="line"><!---->    R' = 0.4 * L + 0.6 * R<!----></span>



<br>





  </tp:docstring>



<span class="line"><!---->  &lt;/tp:docstring&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





  <arg name="num_channels" type="i" direction="in"/>



<span class="line"><!---->  &lt;arg name="num_channels" type="i" direction="in"/&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





  <arg name="coefficient" type="ad" direction="in"/>



<span class="line"><!---->  &lt;arg name="coefficient" type="ad" direction="in"/&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





</method>



<span class="line"><!---->&lt;/method&gt;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





As shown above, CRAS clients in the browser can use this method to set the conversion matrix. The first method parameter num_channels is int32, which presents the matrix's dimensions. The second parameter coefficient is an array composed of multiple doubles that offer every matrix element.



<span class="line"><!---->As shown above, CRAS clients in the browser can use this method to set the conversion matrix. The first method parameter num_channels is int32, which presents the matrix's dimensions. The second parameter coefficient is an array composed of multiple doubles that offer every matrix element.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The bug code relies on handle_set_global_output_channel_remix(). When we received the num_channels and coefficient arguments, we didn't check if num_channels^2 equals the coefficient's size and copied data from the array using num_channels as a counter. So if an attacker sends a big num_channels and a small coefficient array, a heap-over-flow in cras_channel_remix_conv_create() may happen.



<span class="line"><!---->The bug code relies on handle_set_global_output_channel_remix(). When we received the num_channels and coefficient arguments, we didn't check if num_channels^2 equals the coefficient's size and copied data from the array using num_channels as a counter. So if an attacker sends a big num_channels and a small coefficient array, a heap-over-flow in cras_channel_remix_conv_create() may happen.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Control Flow: handle_control_message() -> handle_set_global_output_channel_remix() -> audio_thread_config_global_remix() -> cras_channel_remix_conv_create()



<span class="line"><!---->Control Flow: handle_control_message() -&gt; handle_set_global_output_channel_remix() -&gt; audio_thread_config_global_remix() -&gt; cras_channel_remix_conv_create()<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





struct cras_fmt_conv *cras_channel_remix_conv_create(unsigned int num_channels,



<span class="line"><!---->struct cras_fmt_conv *cras_channel_remix_conv_create(unsigned int num_channels,<!----></span>



<br>





						     const float *coefficient)



<span class="line"><!---->						     const float *coefficient)<!----></span>



<br>





{



<span class="line"><!---->{<!----></span>



<br>





	...



<span class="line"><!---->	...<!----></span>



<br>





	conv->ch_conv_mtx =



<span class="line"><!---->	conv-&gt;ch_conv_mtx =<!----></span>



<br>





		cras_channel_conv_matrix_alloc(num_channels, num_channels);



<span class="line"><!---->		cras_channel_conv_matrix_alloc(num_channels, num_channels);<!----></span>



<br>





	/* Convert the coeffiencnt array to conversion matrix. */



<span class="line"><!---->	/* Convert the coeffiencnt array to conversion matrix. */<!----></span>



<br>





	for (out_ch = 0; out_ch < num_channels; out_ch++)        // <-- num_channels is received from D-Bus without check



<span class="line"><!---->	for (out_ch = 0; out_ch &lt; num_channels; out_ch++)        // &lt;-- num_channels is received from D-Bus without check<!----></span>



<br>





		for (in_ch = 0; in_ch < num_channels; in_ch++)



<span class="line"><!---->		for (in_ch = 0; in_ch &lt; num_channels; in_ch++)<!----></span>



<br>





			conv->ch_conv_mtx[out_ch][in_ch] =



<span class="line"><!---->			conv-&gt;ch_conv_mtx[out_ch][in_ch] =<!----></span>



<br>





				coefficient[in_ch + out_ch * num_channels];  // <-- coefficient is created by calloc(count, sizeof(*coefficient)) where count is received from D-Bus without check, overflow!



<span class="line"><!---->				coefficient[in_ch + out_ch * num_channels];  // &lt;-- coefficient is created by calloc(count, sizeof(*coefficient)) where count is received from D-Bus without check, overflow!<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When we set num_channels not so big, the matrix containing over-flow data on the heap will send to the audio thread in audio_thread_config_global_remix(), which may later help the attacker to get sensitive data or other unexpected results.



<span class="line"><!---->When we set num_channels not so big, the matrix containing over-flow data on the heap will send to the audio thread in audio_thread_config_global_remix(), which may later help the attacker to get sensitive data or other unexpected results.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





ChromiumOS 109.0.5370.0 (Official Build) (64-bit)



<span class="line"><!---->ChromiumOS 109.0.5370.0 (Official Build) (64-bit)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





I built a developer disk image of ChromiumOS and booted it from qemu-kvm with 16GB RAM/8 cores. In ChromiumOS, open a shell and input:



<span class="line"><!---->I built a developer disk image of ChromiumOS and booted it from qemu-kvm with 16GB RAM/8 cores. In ChromiumOS, open a shell and input:<!----></span>



<br>





chronos@localhost ~ $ dbus-send --system --dest=org.chromium.cras --type=method_call --print-reply /org/chromium/cras org.chromium.cras.Control.SetGlobalOutputChannelRemix int32:99999 array:double:9



<span class="line"><!---->chronos@localhost ~ $ dbus-send --system --dest=org.chromium.cras --type=method_call --print-reply /org/chromium/cras org.chromium.cras.Control.SetGlobalOutputChannelRemix int32:99999 array:double:9<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In my case, the CRAS process will crash and report a SEGV exception:

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.
